dark:text-white mb-1 not-first:mt-4"><span class="flex-1">Design patterns</span><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" href="/docs/react/reference/design-patterns/history-patterns"><span class="">History Patterns</span></a></li></ul></details></div></li></ul></div></li></ul><div aria-hidden="true" class="h-12 right-0 sticky bottom-0 left-0 bg-linear-to-t from-white  to-transparent dark:from-stone-950 hidden md:block"></div></div></div></div><div class="md:col-span-8 lg:col-span-9 flex gap-12"><div class="w-full" data-pagefind-body="true" data-pagefind-meta="framework: react"><div class="overflow-hidden pb-8 pt-[calc(61px+2rem)] md:pt-8 md:max-w-3xl mx-auto prose dark:prose-invert dark:prose-code:bg-stone-900"><h1 id="imagedefinition">ImageDefinition</h1>
<p><code>ImageDefinition</code> is a specialized CoValue designed specifically for managing images in Jazz applications. It extends beyond basic file storage by supporting a blurry placeholder, built-in resizing, and progressive loading patterns.</p>
<p>Beyond <code>ImageDefinition</code>, Jazz offers higher-level functions and components that make it easier to use images:</p>
<ul>
<li><a href="#creating-images"><code>createImage()</code></a> - function to create an <code>ImageDefinition</code> from a file</li>
<li><a href="#displaying-images"><code>loadImage</code>, <code>loadImageBySize</code>, <code>highestResAvailable</code></a> - functions to load and display images</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><a href="#displaying-images"><code>Image</code></a> - Component to display an image</li>
</ul>
<p>The <a href="https://github.com/gardencmp/jazz/tree/main/examples/image-upload">Image Upload example</a> demonstrates use of images in Jazz.</p>
<!-- -->
<!-- -->
<!-- -->

                no-underline rounded-b-none border-b-2 transition-colors
                border-transparent hover:border-stone-300 dark:hover:border-stone-600
              " href="/docs/react-native-expo/core-concepts/covalues/imagedef#create-image"><span class="flex items-center grayscale opacity-60"><svg width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 24 22" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M11.39 8.269c.19-.277.397-.312.565-.312.168 0 .447.035.637.312 1.49 2.03 3.95 6.075 5.765 9.06 1.184 1.945 2.093 3.44 2.28 3.63.7.714 1.66.269 2.218-.541.549-.797.701-1.357.701-1.954 0-.407-7.958-15.087-8.759-16.309C14.027.98 13.775.683 12.457.683h-.988c-1.315 0-1.505.297-2.276 1.472C8.392 3.377.433 18.057.433 18.463c0 .598.153 1.158.703 1.955.558.81 1.518 1.255 2.218.54.186-.19 1.095-1.684 2.279-3.63 1.815-2.984 4.267-7.029 5.758-9.06z" class="fill-black dark:fill-white"></path></svg></span>React Native (Expo)</a></div><div><div class="text-stone-500 dark:text-stone-400 p-4 text-center">No content available for tab: </div></div></div>
<p>The <code>createImage()</code> function:</p>
<ul>
<li>Creates an <code>ImageDefinition</code> with the right properties</li>
<li>Optionally generates a small placeholder for immediate display</li>
<li>Creates multiple resolution variants of your image</li>
<li>Returns the created <code>ImageDefinition</code></li>
</ul>
<h3 id="configuration-options" class="group"><a href="#configuration-options" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Configuration Options</span></h3>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">declare</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> function</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> createImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  image</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Blob</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> File</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> string</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  options</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    owner</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Group</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Account</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    placeholder</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> false</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "blur"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    maxSize</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> number</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    progressive</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> boolean</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">)</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Promise</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">Loaded</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">typeof</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> ImageDefinition</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { original</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> }>>;</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="image" class="group"><a href="#image" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>image</code></span></h4>
<p>The image to create an <code>ImageDefinition</code> from.</p>
<p>This can be a <code>Blob</code> or a <code>File</code>.</p>
<!-- -->
<h4 id="owner" class="group"><a href="#owner" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>owner</code></span></h4>
<p>The owner of the <code>ImageDefinition</code>. This is used to control access to the image. See <a href="/docs/react/permissions-and-sharing/overview">Groups as permission scopes</a> for more information on how to use groups to control access to images.</p>
<h4 id="placeholder" class="group"><a href="#placeholder" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>placeholder</code></span></h4>
<p>Disabled by default. This option allows you to automatically generate a low resolution preview for use while the image is loading. Currently, only <code>&quot;blur&quot;</code> is a supported.</p>
<h4 id="maxsize" class="group"><a href="#maxsize" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>maxSize</code></span></h4>
<p>The image generation process includes a maximum size setting that controls the longest side of the image. A built-in resizing feature is applied based on this setting.</p>
<h4 id="progressive" class="group"><a href="#progressive" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>progressive</code></span></h4>
<p>The progressive loading pattern is a technique that allows images to load incrementally, starting with a small version and gradually replacing it with a larger version as it becomes available. This is useful for improving the user experience by showing a placeholder while the image is loading.</p>
<p>Passing <code>progressive: true</code> to <code>createImage()</code> will create internal smaller versions of the image for future uses.</p>
<h3 id="create-multiple-resized-copies" class="group"><a href="#create-multiple-resized-copies" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Create multiple resized copies</span></h3>
<p>To create multiple resized copies of an original image for better layout control, you can use the <code>createImage</code> function multiple times with different parameters for each desired size. Here’s an example of how you might implement this:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { co } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { createImage } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools/media"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// Jazz Schema</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ProductImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.map</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  image</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.image</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  thumbnail</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> co</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.image</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> mainImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> createImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(myBlob);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> thumbnail</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> createImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(myBlob</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  maxSize</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 100</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// or, in case of migration, you can use the original stored image.</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> newThumb</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> createImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(mainImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.original</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.toBlob</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  maxSize</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 100</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> imageSet</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ProductImage</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.create</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  image</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> mainImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  thumbnail</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h3 id="creating-images-on-the-server" class="group"><a href="#creating-images-on-the-server" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Creating images on the server</span></h3>
<p>We provide a <code>createImage</code> function to create images from server side using the same options as the browser version, using the package <code>jazz-tools/media/server</code>. Check the <a href="/docs/react/server-side/setup">server worker</a> documentation to learn more.</p>
<p>The resize features are based on the <code>sharp</code> library, then it is requested as peer dependency in order to use it.</p>
<div id="install-sharp" class="flex flex-col gap-4"><div class="flex gap-1 border-b border-stone-200 dark:border-stone-700"><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-transparent text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 hover:bg-stone-600/10 dark:hover:bg-white/10 active:bg-black/25 dark:active:bg-white/25 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-70 
                rounded-b-none border-b-2 transition-colors
                border-transparent hover:border-stone-300 dark:hover:border-stone-600
              " type="button">npm</button><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-transparent text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 hover:bg-stone-600/10 dark:hover:bg-white/10 active:bg-black/25 dark:active:bg-white/25 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-70 
                rounded-b-none border-b-2 transition-colors
                border-transparent hover:border-stone-300 dark:hover:border-stone-600
              " type="button">pnpm</button></div><div><div class="text-stone-500 dark:text-stone-400 p-4 text-center">No content available for tab: </div></div></div>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { createImage } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools/media/server"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>

<h2 id="displaying-images" class="group"><a href="#displaying-images" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Displaying Images</span></h2>
<p>To use the stored ImageDefinition, there are two ways: declaratively, using the <code>Image</code> component, and imperatively, using the static methods.</p>
<p>The Image component is the best way to let Jazz handle the image loading.</p><h3 id="image-component" class="group"><a href="#image-component" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer"><code>&lt;Image&gt;</code> component</span></h3><div id="image-component" class="flex flex-col gap-4"><div class="flex gap-1 border-b border-stone-200 dark:border-stone-700"><a class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-transparent text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 hover:bg-stone-600/10 dark:hover:bg-white/10 active:bg-black/25 dark:active:bg-white/25 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-70

15.743.303 23.354.883a329 329 0 0 1 12.335 19.695a359 359 0 0 1 11.036 20.54a330 330 0 0 1-11 20.722m22.56-122.124c8.572 4.944 11.906 24.881 6.52 51.026q-.518 2.504-1.15 5.09c-10.622-2.452-22.155-4.275-34.23-5.408c-7.034-10.017-14.323-19.124-21.64-27.008a161 161 0 0 1 5.888-5.4c18.9-16.447 36.564-22.941 44.612-18.3M128 90.808c12.625 0 22.86 10.235 22.86 22.86s-10.235 22.86-22.86 22.86s-22.86-10.235-22.86-22.86s10.235-22.86 22.86-22.86"></path></svg></span>React Native</a><a class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg text-center w-fit text-nowrap text-sm py-1 px-2 bg-transparent text-stone-700 dark:text-stone-100 hover:bg-stone-600/10 dark:hover:bg-white/10 active:bg-black/25 dark:active:bg-white/25 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-70 
                no-underline rounded-b-none border-b-2 transition-colors
                border-transparent hover:border-stone-300 dark:hover:border-stone-600
              " href="/docs/react-native-expo/core-concepts/covalues/imagedef#image-component"><span class="flex items-center grayscale opacity-60"><svg width="1em" height="1em" viewBox="0 0 24 22" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M11.39 8.269c.19-.277.397-.312.565-.312.168 0 .447.035.637.312 1.49 2.03 3.95 6.075 5.765 9.06 1.184 1.945 2.093 3.44 2.28 3.63.7.714 1.66.269 2.218-.541.549-.797.701-1.357.701-1.954 0-.407-7.958-15.087-8.759-16.309C14.027.98 13.775.683 12.457.683h-.988c-1.315 0-1.505.297-2.276 1.472C8.392 3.377.433 18.057.433 18.463c0 .598.153 1.158.703 1.955.558.81 1.518 1.255 2.218.54.186-.19 1.095-1.684 2.279-3.63 1.815-2.984 4.267-7.029 5.758-9.06z" class="fill-black dark:fill-white"></path></svg></span>React Native (Expo)</a></div><div><div class="text-stone-500 dark:text-stone-400 p-4 text-center">No content available for tab: </div></div></div><p>The <code>Image</code> component handles:</p><ul>
<li>Showing a placeholder while loading, if generated or specified</li>
<li>Automatically selecting the appropriate resolution, if generated with progressive loading</li>
<li>Progressive enhancement as higher resolutions become available, if generated with progressive loading</li>
<li>Determining the correct width/height attributes to avoid layout shifting</li>
<li>Cleaning up resources when unmounted</li>
</ul><p>The component&#x27;s props are:</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">export</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> type</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> ImageProps</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Omit</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">  HTMLImgAttributes</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">  "src"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "srcset"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "width"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "height"</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">> </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">&#x26;</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> number</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "original"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> number</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> |</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "original"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  placeholder</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">?:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> string</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">};</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<!-- -->
<h4 id="width-and-height-props" class="group"><a href="#width-and-height-props" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Width and Height props</span></h4><p>The <code>width</code> and <code>height</code> props are used to control the best resolution to use but also the width and height attributes of the image tag.</p><p>Let&#x27;s say we have an image with a width of 1920px and a height of 1080px.</p><div class="[&amp;_span]:whitespace-normal not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> /></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">      // Image with the highest resolution available</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"original"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"original"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> /></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">      // Image with width 1920 and height 1080</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">{</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">} /></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">      // Better to avoid, as may be rendered with 0 height</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">{</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">} </span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"original"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> /></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">      // Keeps the aspect ratio (height: 338)</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"original"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">{</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">} /></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">      // As above, aspect ratio is maintained, width is 1067</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">      &#x3C;</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">{</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">} </span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">{</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">} /></span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">      // Renders as a 600x600 square</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div><p>If the image was generated with progressive loading, the <code>width</code> and <code>height</code> props will determine the best resolution to use.</p>
<h4 id="lazy-loading" class="group"><a href="#lazy-loading" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Lazy loading</span></h4><p>The <code>Image</code> component supports lazy loading with the [same options as the native browser <code>loading</code> attribute].(https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/HTML/Reference/Elements/img#loading). It will generate the blob url for the image when the browser&#x27;s viewport reaches the image.</p><div class="[&amp;_span]:whitespace-normal not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">&#x3C;</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">Image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> imageId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"original"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"original"</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> loading</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"lazy"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> /></span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h4 id="placeholder" class="group"><a href="#placeholder" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Placeholder</span></h4><p>You can choose to specify a custom placeholder to display as a fallback while an image is loading in case your image does not have a placeholder generated. A data URL or a URL for a static asset works well here.</p><h3 id="imperative-usage" class="group"><a href="#imperative-usage" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Imperative Usage</span></h3>
<p>Like other CoValues, <code>ImageDefinition</code> can be used to load the object.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> image</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ImageDefinition</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.load</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"123"</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  resolve</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    original</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> true</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">image</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.$isLoaded) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    originalSize</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> image</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.originalSize</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    placeholderDataUrl</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> image</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.placeholderDataURL</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    original</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> image</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.original</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA"> // this FileStream may be not loaded yet</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p><code>image.original</code> is a <code>FileStream</code> and its content can be read as described in the <a href="/docs/react/core-concepts/covalues/filestreams#reading-from-filestreams">FileStream</a> documentation.</p>
<p>Since FileStream objects are also CoValues, they must be loaded before use. To simplify loading, if you want to load the binary data saved as Original, you can use the <code>loadImage</code> function.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { loadImage } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools/media"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> loadedImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> loadImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(imageDefinitionOrId);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (loadedImage </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">===</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> null</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  throw</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Error</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"Image not found"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> img</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> document</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.createElement</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"img"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.width </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> loadedImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.width;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.height </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> loadedImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.height;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.src </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> URL</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.createObjectURL</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">loadedImage</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.toBlob</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">()</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">onload</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> () </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> URL</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.revokeObjectURL</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.src);</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>If the image was generated with progressive loading, and you want to access the best-fit resolution, use <code>loadImageBySize</code>. It will load the image of the best resolution that fits the wanted width and height.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { loadImageBySize } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools/media"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> imageLoadedBySize</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> loadImageBySize</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(imageDefinitionOrId</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 600</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">); </span><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// 600x600</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (imageLoadedBySize) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  console</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.log</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> imageLoadedBySize</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.width</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> imageLoadedBySize</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.height</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    image</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> imageLoadedBySize</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.image</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  });</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<p>If want to dynamically listen to the <em>loaded</em> resolution that best fits the wanted width and height, you can use the <code>subscribe</code> and the <code>highestResAvailable</code> function.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { highestResAvailable } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools/media"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> progressiveImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> await</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> ImageDefinition</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.load</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(imageId);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">!</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">progressiveImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.$isLoaded) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  throw</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> new</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> Error</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"Image not loaded"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> img</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> document</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.createElement</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69">"img"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.width </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.height </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// start with the placeholder</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">progressiveImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.placeholderDataURL) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">  img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.src </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> progressiveImage</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.placeholderDataURL;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">}</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">// then listen to the image changes</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">progressiveImage</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">$jazz</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.subscribe</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({}</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (image) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> bestImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> highestResAvailable</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(image</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 600</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> 600</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">);</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">  if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (bestImage) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">    // bestImage is again a FileStream</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> blob</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> bestImage</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">image</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.toBlob</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">();</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">    if</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (blob) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">      const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> url</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> URL</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.createObjectURL</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(blob);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">      img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.src </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> url;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9">      img</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">.</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">onload</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> () </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> URL</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">.revokeObjectURL</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">(url);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">    }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">});</span></span></code></pre></div></pre></div>
<h2 id="custom-image-manipulation-implementations" class="group"><a href="#custom-image-manipulation-implementations" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Custom image manipulation implementations</span></h2>
<p>To manipulate images (like placeholders, resizing, etc.), <code>createImage()</code> uses different implementations depending on the environment.</p>
<p>On the browser, image manipulation is done using the <code>canvas</code> API.</p>
<!-- -->
<!-- -->
<p>If you want to use a custom implementation, you can use the <code>createImageFactory</code> function in order create your own <code>createImage</code> function and use your preferred image manipulation library.</p>
<div class="not-prose group relative"><pre class="h-full overflow-x-auto border rounded-md p-0 bg-stone-50 dark:bg-stone-925 text-black dark:text-white text-sm"><div><pre class="shiki shiki-themes jazz-light jazz-dark" style="background-color:#fffffe;--shiki-dark-bg:#1e1e1e;color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#d1d1d1" tabindex="0" add="" del=""><code><span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">import</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> { createImageFactory } </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">from</span><span style="color:#42BB69;--shiki-dark:#42BB69"> "jazz-tools/media"</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">;</span></span>
<span class="line"></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">const</span><span style="color:#00A5A5;--shiki-dark:#2DC9C9"> customCreateImage</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> =</span><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF"> createImageFactory</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">({</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#445DD7;--shiki-dark:#9BABFF">  createFileStreamFromSource</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">:</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF"> async</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> (source</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> owner) </span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#7B8BFF">=></span><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1"> {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">    // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#333333;--shiki-dark:#D1D1D1">  }</span><span style="color:#7B8BFF;--shiki-dark:#BBBBBB">,</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#AAA;--shiki-dark:#AAA">    // ...</span></span>

<h2 id="best-practices" class="group"><a href="#best-practices" class="no-underline float-left absolute -ml-[1.25em] hidden sm:block opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity" aria-label="Navigate to header" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><span aria-hidden="true">#</span></a><span class="cursor-pointer">Best Practices</span></h2>
<ul>
<li><strong>Set image sizes</strong> when possible to avoid layout shifts</li>
<li><strong>Use placeholders</strong> (like LQIP - Low Quality Image Placeholders) for instant rendering</li>
<li><strong>Prioritize loading</strong> the resolution appropriate for the current viewport</li>
<li><strong>Consider device pixel ratio</strong> (window.devicePixelRatio) for high-DPI displays</li>
<li><strong>Always call URL.revokeObjectURL</strong> after the image loads to prevent memory leaks</li>
</ul><div class="flex flex-row justify-start flex-wrap items-center gap-2 py-2"><strong>Was this page helpful?</strong><div><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center gap-2 rounded-lg
